| <span data-ttu-id="0b49b-454">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b49b-454">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="0b49b-455">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b49b-455">Value</span></span> |
